RaxML-style partition definitions
Warning: RAxML allows for only a single model of rate heterogeneity in partitioned analyses. I.e. all partitions must be assigned one of three types of model: No heterogeneity (e.g. GTR); +G (e.g. GTR+G); or +I+G (e.g. GTR+I+G). If the best models for your datasetcontain different types of model for different subsets you will need to decide on the best rate heterogeneity model before you run RAxML. If you prefer to do things more rigorously, you can run separate PartitionFinder analyses for each type of rate heterogenetity Then choose the scheme with the lowest AIC/AICc/BIC score. Note that these re-runs will be quick!

	lset applyto=(402) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(403) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(404) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(405) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(406) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(407) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(408) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(409) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(410) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(411) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(412) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(413) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(414) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(415) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(416) nst=6 rates=gamma;
	lset applyto=(417) nst=6 rates=gamma;

	prset applyto=(all) ratepr=variable;
	unlink statefreq=(all) revmat=(all) shape=(all) pinvar=(all) tratio=(all);

end;
